31/01/23, 14:13 - Pallavi Bangale Ma'am PVGCOET: Dear PVG's COET students, 

Please note that *tonight, 11.59pm* is the *deadline* at *PVG's COET* to apply for the *Finlatics Startup Strategist Program* an *Online Live Project* that helps students gain *Work Experience* in *building, launching & scaling a start-up*.

On this project, you'll work on start-up ideas across sectors like *EV's*, *digital media & OTT*, and *sustainable & consumer tech* to develop business models, create *roadmaps* for *product development* & *minimum viable product launch*; and prepare *pitches* for investment. 

At the end of this program you will get: 
- *Certificate of Work Experience*
- *Letter of Recommendation* on performance

To apply, you can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba-application/application/index.php?utm_src=sspvgcoetwd

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of this project. 

*Project Duration* : 2 months

*Project Start*: Flexible on your schedule. 

You can also take a *break* for exams, assignments or personal commitment as well as take an *extension* if you cannot complete it within the duration. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee: Rs. 1499 + GST

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement,
Team Finlatics
Know more about us: https://www.finlatics.com/
Visit us on LinkedIn: https://www.linkedin.com/company/fincrux-enabling-insights/

03/02/23, 14:27 - +91 70218 09557: ğŸ‡ğŸ† *RANASANGRAM* ğŸ†ğŸ‡
It brings us great pleasure to cordially invite you all to PVG's COET and GKPIOM's very own sports fest, *Ranasangram'23*. 

Ranasangram is an *Inter Department* event where students from each year of various departments can form a team and compete in various sports events to win prizes, medals and certificates.

This is our college sports event and not the selection trials for the college team. Matches will be played between individual classes according to the draws made by respective coordinators. The matches may be between teams from the same or different departments.

Make your own teams in your class and then, *only the captain of the team for every sport from each class should contact the coordinators.* 

This event will be consisting of exciting sports such as:
1. Cricket(M/W)
2. Football(M)
3. Volleyball(M/W)
4. Basketball(M/W)
5. Kabaddi(M)
6. Badminton(M/W/MEN'S DOUBLES/WOMEN'S DOUBLES)
7. Chess(M/W)
8. Athletics(M/W)
9. Table tennis(M/W)
10. Dodgeball(W)


*NOTE:*
*For boys, combined teams from FE, SE, TE, BE are not allowed.*
*If the girls team is short of players then they are allowed to form a combined team (FE, SE, TE, BE) but of the same department.*
*The departments having 2 divisions like Mech and E&TC are instructed to make a single team (Eg. select the best players from both divisions)*

*STUDENTS WILL NOT BE ALLOWED TO TAKE PART IN THE SPORTS EVENTS IF THE CONSENT FORMS ARE NOT SUBMITTED AT THE TIME OF THE EVENT.*



*Venue: PVG's COET and GKPIOM ground*
*Dates: 9th - 11th February 2023* 

*May the best department win*ğŸ’¯ 

Instagram link: https://instagram.com/pvgcoet.sports?igshid=NDk5N2NlZjQ=

*Technical dumb charades*

â°Time Slot:- 12 pm to 1:30 pm

ğŸ“ŒRules:
1. The team should be of 2-3 members.
2. The time limit will be  3 min.
3. One member acts out a word or phrase without speaking, while the others try to guess what it is.
4. No speaking, or sounds are allowed, only gestures and facial expressions.
6.Teams take turns acting out words or phrases, and each correct guess earns a point for the team.
7. The game has a Time Limit of  3 mins , with each team having a limited amount of time to act out as many words or phrases as possible.
8. The team with the most points at the end of the game wins.
9. Any member of the team can act, but only one member can act at a time.
10. If a team takes too long to guess the word or phrase, or if the actor breaks any of the rules, the turn moves on to the next team.

08/09/23, 22:59 - Dr Minakshi Pradeep Atre Pvg: Dear all,  

World EV Day is a global celebration that takes place annually on September 9th, where people from around the world come together to raise awareness of electric vehicles and the ways that they can benefit us and our environment.

This year,  On  9 th September 2023, PVG's COET & GKPIOM, Pune (Department of Electrical Engineering along with Energy Club) is celebrating it by doing Inauguration of
"Green Electric Two Wheeler Solar PV Charging Station",  on the occasion of

Ã˜  The top 35 teams (30 Shortlisted + 5 waitlisted) nominations (qualified through an internal hackathon conducted by institute at their premise) must be submitted on the SIH portal by the College SPOC only. 

Ã˜  How to form a team?

o   All team members should be from the same college/school; no inter-college/school teams will be allowed. However, for college/ institute; members from different branches of the will be encouraged to form a team.

o   Each team would mandatorily comprise of 6 members including the team leader and at least one female member.

o   As the software edition of the hackathon is a digital product development competition, the majority of the team members MUST be well versed with programming skills. For the hardware edition, we encourage multi-disciplinary teams ï¿½ which means your team should have a good mix of Mechanical Engineers, Electronic Engineers, Product Designers and Programmers, etc.

 

Ã˜  A team will not be able to make multiple idea submissions.

 

Ã˜  The Participating Team can nominate up to two mentors who can be any senior faculty and domain expert that will guide the team and nurture their idea.

The Internship Permission Letter for 2023 is now available for distribution. To obtain a PDF copy of the permission letter, kindly send an email to my official email address provided below. I will attach the permission letter to the same email.

1.Subject of email: Full Name of the Student, Class, and Purpose

1.Industry Name

3.Period of Internship in Days
4.Online or Offline

1.Print two color copies of the letter.
2.Complete the necessary details on both copies, including the recipient's details from the industry, the number of students, and the name(s) of the student(s).
3.The letter bears the official seal of the College along with the signatures of the Principal Sir and the department coordinator.

03/01/24, 10:58 - Prof. Vijayalaxmi Kanade Teacher pvg: *AMCAT assessment test for TE on 12th Jan 2024*
Pre-registration is mandatory in following Google form
https://forms.gle/kzzsyLB8aJDuJaet7

The college will pay the fees for first 400 registrations.

*What is AMCAT*
AMCAT is an employability assessment test. The score generated is widely accepted by the recruiters. Also the details analysis will be given to each student who appeared for the test.

The total time for various sections will be approx. 3 hours. You have to give these tests from college labs in your dept. Time and Venue will be conveyed to you.

*Modules for the test:*
1.	English -18 Min (18 Q)
2.	Logical-15 Min (12 Q)
3.	Quantitative Ability-20 Min (16 Q)
4.	Personality Assessment (AMPI)- 15 Min
5.	Skill/Domain test: 20 Min
6.	Spoken English test: 20 Min (from home afterwards)
7.	Writex: 25 Min
8.	Excel: 10 Min
9.	Interview Assessment: 25 Min (from home afterwards)
10.	Coding: 20 Min
11.	Debugging: 20 Min

*Benefits of the AMCAT Tests*
1.	Students will get detail analysis about above skills and identify the scope for improvements.
2.Students can directly apply for the jobs available on https://www.myamcat.com/ portal
3.	Overall employability will be enhanced.
4.	Top performers can showcase/send their scores to different dream companies.

11/01/24, 16:14 - Prof. Vijayalaxmi Kanade Teacher pvg: *General Instructions for AMCAT Test:*
1.	Test time and venue will be conveyed by the dept.

2.	Exam will be conducted in college Labs only. (No exam from home)
3. If there is any problem with lab machine or no.of machines are less, then you may be allowed to use your laptop and self hotspot connection. 
4.	username and password are separate for each student, and will be provided at the time of exam.
5.	Usernames are branch-wise, accordingly you will get questions. So check once whether you got your branch username.
6.	Link for exam:
https://amcatcampus.aspiringminds.com/
7.	No negative marking.
8.	Calculators are *not allowed* during the test.
9.	Do not minimize test window, do not open any other tab in system once the test starts. If you try to do so, you will get warning and in further attempts test will get logged-out.
10.	You can't switch between the question and modules, that means question no. 1 needs to attempt first then second and so on.
11.	Module-wise timer will be displayed.
12.	You cannot carry remaining time from first module to second module
13.	Coding test is available for all branches, but scorecard gives module-wise score, So if you are not good in coding, that will not affect other module scores.

ğŸ‡ğŸ† RANSANGRAM ğŸ†ğŸ‡
It brings us great pleasure to cordially invite you all to PVG's COET and GKPIOM's very own sports fest, Ransangram'24. 

Ransangram is an Inter Department event where students from each year of various departments can form a team and compete in various sports events to win prizes, medals and certificates.

This is our college sports event and not the selection trials for the college team. Matches will be played between individual classes according to the draws made by respective coordinators. The matches may be between teams from the same or different departments.

Make your own teams in your class and then, only the captain or representative of the team for every sport from each class should contact the coordinators or register for the event. 

This event will be consisting of exciting sports such as:
1. Cricket(M/W/Staff)
2. Football(M)
3. Volleyball(M/W)
4. Basketball(M/W)
5. Kabaddi(M)
6. Badminton(M/W)
7. Chess(M/W/Staff)
8. Athletics(M/W)
9. Table tennis(M/W singles and Men's doubles)
10. Dodgeball(W)
11. Shot put(M/W)
12. Powerlifting(M/W)

*NOTE:*
*For boys, combined teams from FE, SE, TE, BE are not allowed except for AI&DS and MBA department.*
*If the girls team is short of players then they are allowed to form a combined team (FE, SE, TE, BE) but of the same department.*
*The departments having 2 divisions like Mech and E&TC are instructed to make a single team (Eg. select the best players from both divisions)*


*STUDENTS WILL NOT BE ALLOWED TO TAKE PART IN THE SPORTS EVENTS IF THE CONSENT FORMS ARE NOT SUBMITTED AT THE TIME OF THE EVENT.*

AY 2023-24

You know that, In-sem Exam of Sem II is starting from 20th March 2024. In the morning FE & TE exams will be from 11am to 12noon and SE & BE exams will be from 2pm to 3pm.
These exams will be as per your 1st semester exam seat number, please note. 

Remember the following things while appearing for the exam:
1. You may not be allowed to appear for the exam is till today, you have:
a. Not filled MAHA DBT Samajkalyan form till date
b.  Not fulfil documents requirement of the college office and hence your form is incomplete / not forwarded by the college
c.  Exam form not filled / submitted to the college
d.  SC category scholarship students received 60% fees from government to their account but amount is not paid / reimbursed to college till date
2. This time there will be two students of different branch and year will seat on one bench for the exam
3. Daily seating arrangement will change and will be available on your email id around 30 - 35 minutes before the scheduled time of exam
4. Try to bring least writing material with you for exam
5. You will not be allowed to go out of the exam hall during the entire exam period (even for Bio Break)
6. I-Card Compulsory during exam. Digital wrist watch not be allowed in exam hall
7. You will not wear CAP, sweater, jerkin, shoes, sandals, scarf etc during exam
8. Exchange of any kind of material (writing, drawing etc) not allowed
9. As per new SPPU norms, no supplement will be issued to student in any condition, please note
10. Writing on the classroom walls, benches is strictly prohibited (classrooms are recently painted from NAAC and NBA point of view

Greetings from Industry Institute Cell.

Pls go through the TNS India Foundation program details of C2TC (Campus to Technical Careers) program and eligible students please register accordingly. The training will start from June second week.

 C2TC Program is intended to assist college graduates from specific branches - to be employment ready for careers in technical (programming, software, IT related) roles in IT/ITES and allied organisations in the formal sector. This program implemented by TNS India Foundation (TNSIF) is supported by some of the largest corporate organizations in the IT/ ITeS and allied sectors under their CSR initiatives.


I am herewith attaching TNS India Foundation's C2TC Program Details for your perusal. 



 Eligibility criteria:

1. Family income of the student should be less than 5 Lakhs per year.

2. Highest qualification of the student can be BE/B.Tech (CS/IT/ECE/EEE) and MCA/MSc (IT/CS)

3. Year of passing for the highest qualification is 2025

4. The student should be a job seeker and willing to take up an IT sector job immediately after graduation.

5. Students who have plans to take up higher education after graduation and students who already have a job offer are not eligible.

6. The training and placement assistance is free of cost

7. Upon screening tests in the first 4 days, you will be incubated free of cost training and placement assistance.



 Ps.: - This communication is not linked to any commercial expectations from our side, either from candidates or any educational institutes.


Going forward, the students must register on the following orientation link

06/07/24, 17:22 - Prof. Vijayalaxmi Kanade Teacher pvg: We are conducting Online pre-training assessment today,
All registered students must have got email from Talent Battle.

Steps to access the *Pre Assessment Test for PVG*

Please read all the instructions, steps are very easy to access the test.

Steps to appear for the test:

Use your email id. In case of a password problem, click on the forgot password on our website.

1) Click on https://talentbattle.in/login

2) If you don't know password, use forgot password option.

3)  The dashboard will be opened. Click on the Mock Tests.

4)Click on Pre Assessment Test

Click *Technical Pre Assessment Test* (questions IT based., So if Core branch students are not comfortable, they can avoid... though it is recommended to try)

Click - *Aptitude Pre Assessment Test*

*Note* - You can start with any of the Assessment First but once you start need to complete. Assessments have the timers and once the duration is completed it will be submitted Automatically. 

*Do Not* start both the tests simultaneously. You need to complete 1 test at a time.  

5) You can check the duration and maximum marks for the test. Click on *Give test to start the test.* 

6) Instructions will be displayed. Then at the bottom side, *click on Start Now.*

7) Pop up will come, Click on *Yes to start the test*

Note - For any Technical support during the assessment you can write to contact@talentbattle.in

05/09/24, 14:58 - Prof. Vijayalaxmi Kanade Teacher pvg: Dear Students,
 

Greetings!

Principal Global Test is scheduled for 9th Sept 2024; 11:00 am to 1:00 pm.
PFA the list of 178 candidates the company has shortlisted for the test.

 

HirePro Team will initiate the test registration process (on the day before i.e. on 8/9/24 or on the 9th Morning itself before the test. Tgv hhe students will have to be vigilant and check their email accordingly).


Please find below important instructions & other details for the online test. 

* It will be a proctored test and students can take the same from their own place. 
* Smooth Internet connectivity is most important for the test as 99% problems that occur during the test are due to bandwith issue. Hence students will have to ensure full battery and data back-up with adequate internet speed during the test.
* Please be advised that in the event of any issues arising from an internet connection, the test will not be restarted or rescheduled under any circumstances. Therefore, it is essential to ensure a stable internet connection.  

Test duration : 2 hours.
Test comprises : Aptitude, English, Technical & Coding (Option to choose either 1 â€“ C/C++/Java/Python)
 
System Requirements for Taking the Test:
You will need a webcam and microphone enabled laptop or desktop to take the test. DO NOT take the test on a mobile device.
Use the updated version of Google Chrome (latest Version - excluding the Beta Version) for the best performance.
Ensure your system "Clock dateâ€ and "Time" are updated and synced with your location time zone.
Minimum hardware requirement of the system: RAM - 4 GB, Processor - i3 dual core 2.2 Ghz 5th Generation or equivalent/higher.
Ensure that the minimum speed of the internet connection is 2 Mbps (Both Upload & Download speed should be 2 MBPS or More)
Preferably use LAN or WiFi network connectivity.
Close all background applications that may trigger any system pop-ups (Outlook, other email clients, Anti-virus, Instant Messengers, News-Notifications, Other browsers/tabs, etc).
Ensure that Microphone and Webcam are connected to the system & access is allowed in the browser. 
If blocked, follow these steps: Go to Chrome > Settings > Advanced > Privacy and Security > Content Settings > Enable Microphone and Camera
Camera Check Link: https://webcamtests.com/
Microphone Check Link: https://www.onlinemictest.com/
Instructions for the test:
Make sure you are in a stress-free environment with no disturbances and ample time in hand before starting the test.
Keep your laptop plugged into the main power while taking the test.
This test is video & audio proctored. During the test, your video and audio are recorded and analyzed to maintain the integrity of the test. DO NOT attempt to cheat in any way else you will be immediately disqualified.
Access this test in a well-lit and quiet environment. Ensure that you are facing towards the light source.
While taking the test do not move away from the test window to any other application without submitting or completing the test. The test will be automatically submitted if you try to move out of the test window repeatedly.
Keep a pen-paper handy for rough work. 
Use of calculators and mobile phones is not permitted during the test.
Mobile phones can be used only to reach out to the support team for any technical difficulties.
Once you are ready, click the test link given, enter your user ID & password mentioned in the body of the email and click on the Login button.
The page will check for camera, browser, and microphone availability and compatibility. Once all are OK, you will be prompted to take a selfie.
Take a selfie by clicking on the Camera button. Click on the Continue button after taking a selfie where your face is clearly visible.
The page will load with the Test details & Test Instructions. Read and understand all of them carefully.
There will be a checkbox with "I Agree to the Terms and Conditions". Once you check this, the Start Test button will be enabled. Click on the â€œStart Test'' button to start taking the test.
A timer is displayed on the top right corner of the window throughout the test. This timer indicates the remaining time.
Once you reach the last question, the â€œEnd Testâ€ button will be enabled at the bottom of the page. Once you have answered the questions you can submit your test. Confirm by clicking on the â€œI am done with the testâ€ button.
Once you submit the test you will be shown a completion message and can safely close the browser window.
Important Note:
Make sure to restart your machine & internet connection before you start the test
Please close all the other applications, and disable all Chrome extensions
 
The virtual Pre-Placement Talk (PPT) Session is scheduled on the next day i.e. on Tue, 10th Sept. at 11:00am, we will share the Teams link on Mon 9th Sept 1st half.
 
Best Regards,
Industry-Institute Cell.
